## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task models population growth rate dP/dt as a function of time t and population P, which is the canonical form of population dynamics ODEs. The relationship likely involves density-dependent growth mechanisms such as logistic growth, Allee effects, or time-varying carrying capacities.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Exponential (Malthusian) growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (density-independent growth)
- Logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) (density-dependent growth with carrying capacity)
- Gompertz growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P) (growth rate decreases logarithmically with population)
- Theta-logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (generalized logistic with shape parameter)
- Allee effect (strong): dP_dt = c0 * P * (P * c1 - 1) * (1 - c2 * P) (growth negative below threshold)
- Allee effect (weak): dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 * (1 - c2 * P) (power-law density dependence at low population)
- Beverton-Holt continuous: dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (saturating per-capita growth)
- Time-varying logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (1 + c2 * t) (logistic with time-dependent carrying capacity)
- Periodic environment: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (1 + c2 * sin(c3 * t)) (seasonal variation in growth)
- Richards growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) * c3 (flexible sigmoid growth model)
- Harvesting model: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 * P (logistic growth with proportional harvesting)
- Logarithmic correction: dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P * log(P) (Gompertz-type reformulation)
- Polynomial density dependence: dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2 + c2 * P**3 (cubic growth model with multiple equilibria)
- Time-decay growth rate: dP_dt = c0 * P * exp(c1 * t) (exponentially changing intrinsic growth rate)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Density-dependent regulation → multiplicative factor (1 - P/K) or rational forms P/(1+P) reducing per-capita growth at high density
- Allee effects (minimum viable population) → quadratic or cubic terms in P creating an unstable lower equilibrium point
- Gompertz-type growth → log(P) terms indicating per-capita growth rate decreases logarithmically with population size
- Seasonality or periodic forcing → trigonometric functions of time sin(c*t) or cos(c*t) modulating growth parameters
- Multiple stable equilibria → cubic or higher-order polynomial terms in P creating multiple zero-crossings in dP/dt
- Per-capita growth rate structure → dP/dt should factor as P * f(P, t), ensuring dP/dt = 0 when P = 0 (extinction is a fixed point)
- Time-dependent carrying capacity → interaction terms between t and P such as t*P or P*exp(c*t) indicating environmental change
- Compensatory vs depensatory mortality → sign and order of P^n terms distinguish stabilizing from destabilizing density effects

GT = C*P^(1/3) + (A + C + C)*P - (C/c4)*P²

**Candidate 38:** c0 + c1*(P+c2)^(1/3) + c3*exp(P*c4). Set c3=0, c0=0, c2=0: c1*P^(1/3). Missing P, P². **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 39:** P^(4/3)*c0 + P^(1/3)*c1/(P*c2+c3) + P*c4/(P*c2+c3). Set c2=0: P^(4/3)*c0 + c1*P^(1/3)/c3 + c4*P/c3. Has P^(4/3). Set c0=0: c1*P^(1/3)/c3 + c4*P/c3. Missing P². **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 40:** P^(1/3)*c0 + P^(1/3)*c1/(P*c2+c3) + P*c4/(P*c2+c3). Set c2=0: c0*P^(1/3) + c1*P^(1/3)/c3 + c4*P/c3 = (c0+c1/c3)*P^(1/3) + (c4/c3)*P. Missing P². **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 41:** (P^(4/3)*c0 + P^(1/3)*c3 + P*c4 + P*c5)/(P*c1+c2). Set c1=0: (c0*P^(4/3) + c3*P^(1/3) + (c4+c5)*P)/c2. Has P^(4/3). Set c0=0: (c3*P^(1/3) + (c4+c5)*P)/c2. Missing P². **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 42:** (P^(4/3)*c0 + P^(1/3)*c3 + P*c4)/(P*c1+c2). Set c1=0: same as above with c0→can be 0. Missing P². **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 43:** P^(1/3)*c0 + P*c1 + c2*sin(P*c3+c4) + c5*sin(P*c6+c7). Set c2=0, c5=0. Missing P². **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 44:** Has t and exp. Set t terms to 0, exp to 0. Rational terms: P*c1/(P*c2+c3) + c8/(P*c2+c3). Set c2=0: c1*P/c3 + c8/c3. Plus c0*P + c4*(P+c5)^(1/3). Set c5=0: c4*P^(1/3). Total: (c0+c1/c3)*P + c4*P^(1/3) + c8/c3. Missing P². **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 45:** P^(7/3)*c0 + P^(4/3)*c1 + P^(1/3)*c2 + P*c3 + c4*log(P*c5+1). Set c0=0, c1=0, c4=0. = c2*P^(1/3) + c3*P. Missing P². **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 46:** Has t. Set t terms to 0 (c3=0, c6=0). c1*exp(P*c2) + c7. Set c1=0: c0*P^(1/3) + c7. Missing P, P². **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 47:** P*c0 + P*c1*(P*c2)^c3 + c4*log(P*c5+1). = P*c0 + c1*c2^c3*P^(1+c3) + c4*log(...). Set c4=0. Set c3=1: P² term + P. Missing P^(1/3). Set c3=-2/3: P^(1/3) + P. Missing P². **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 48:** P^(1/3)*c0 + c1*exp(P*c2) + c3. Set c1=0: c0*P^(1/3) + c3. Missing P, P². **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 49:** Has t. P*c0 + P*(P*c1)^c2 + c3 + c4*t*(P+c5)^c6. Set c4=0: P*c0 + c1^c2*P^(1+c2) + c3. Same issue as before - can only get one extra power. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 50:** Has t. P^(1/3)*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*(c3+t)^c4 + c5*t*(P+c6)^c7. The t-dependent terms can't all be zeroed while keeping P². Set c5=0, c4=0: P*c2*1 = c2*P. Total: c0*P^(1/3) + (c1+c2)*P. Missing P². **NO MATCH**
